    if (opts.isDdInT1) {
      $SearchJS.when('search-js-autocomplete').run('autocomplete-dd-init', function(){ searchDropdown(); });
    }

  } // END conditional for window.$SearchJS

  
  
  function initializeAutocomplete(jQuery) {
    
    var issInitObj = buildIssInitObject(opts, issOpts);

    tryInitClientTriggeredWeblabs(issInitObj);
  } // END initializeAutocomplete

  
  
  function tryInitClientTriggeredWeblabs(issInitObj) {
    
    if (opts.isDoCtw) {
      $SearchJS.importEvent('search-csl');
      $SearchJS.when('search-csl').run('autocomplete-csl-init', function delegateToInitSearchCsl(searchCSL) { initSearchCsl( searchCSL, issInitObj ); } );
    } else {
      $SearchJS.declare('canCreateAutocomplete', issInitObj);
    }
  }

  
  
  function initSearchCsl(searchCSL, issInitObject) {
    searchCSL.init(opts.pageType, (window.ue && window.ue.rid) || opts.requestId);

    
    var keydownCtw = opts.keydownTriggeredWeblabs;
    var displayCtw = opts.displayTriggeredWeblabs;

    
    issInitObject.doCTWKeydown = function(e) {
        for (var i = 0; i < keydownCtw.length; i++) {
          searchCSL.addWlt(keydownCtw[i].call ? keydownCtw[i](e) : keydownCtw[i]);
        }
      };

    issInitObject.doCTWDisplay = function(data) {
        for (var i = 0; i < displayCtw.length; i++) {
          searchCSL.addWlt(displayCtw[i].call ? displayCtw[i](data) : displayCtw[i]);
        }
      };

    $SearchJS.declare('canCreateAutocomplete', issInitObject);
  } // END initSearchCsl

  
  
  function createAutocomplete(issObject) {
    iss = new AutoComplete(issObject);

    $SearchJS.publish('search-js-autocomplete', iss);

    logMetrics();
  } // END createAutocomplete

  
  
  function buildIssInitObject(opts, issOpts, isNewIss) {
    var issInitObj = {
        src: opts.host
      , sessionId: opts.sessionId
      , requestId: opts.requestId
      , mkt: opts.marketId
      , obfMkt: opts.obfuscatedMarketId
      , pageType: opts.pageType
      , language: opts.language
      , aliases: opts.searchAliases
      , fb: issOpts.fallbackFlag
      , isDigitalFeaturesEnabled: issOpts.isDigitalFeaturesEnabled
      , isWayfindingEnabled: issOpts.isWayfindingEnabled
      , issPrimeEligible: issOpts.issPrimeEligible
      , deptText: issOpts.departmentText
      , sugText: issOpts.suggestionText
      , filterAliases: opts.filterAliases
      , emphasizeSuggestionsTreatment: issOpts.emphasizeSuggestionsTreatment
      , crossCategoryEmphasisTreatment: issOpts.crossCategoryEmphasisTreatment
      , showSuggestionsOnSearchboxFocusTreatment: issOpts.showSuggestionsOnSearchboxFocusTreatment
      , issAfterNCharsTreatment: issOpts.issAfterNCharsTreatment
      , issRelatedSearchesTreatment: issOpts.issRelatedSearchesTreatment
      , recentSearchesTreatment: issOpts.recentSearchesTreatment
      , recentSearchesText: issOpts.recentSearchesText
      , cf: issOpts.cf
      , ime: opts.isJpOrCn
      , mktid: opts.marketId
      , qs: opts.isJpOrCn
      , issCorpus: issOpts.issCorpus
      , deepNodeISS: {
          searchAliasAccessor: function($) {
            return (window.SearchPageAccess && window.SearchPageAccess.searchAlias()) ||
                   $('select.searchSelect').children().attr('data-root-alias');
          },
          searchAliasDisplayNameAccessor: function() {
            return (window.SearchPageAccess && window.SearchPageAccess.searchAliasDisplayName());
          }
        }
    };

    // If we aren't using the new ISS then we need to add these properties
    if (!isNewIss) {
      issInitObj.dd = issOpts.dropdown; // The element with id searchDropdownBox doesn't exist in C.
      issInitObj.imeSpacing = issOpts.imeSpacing;
      issInitObj.isNavInline = 1;
      issInitObj.triggerISSOnClick = 0;
      issInitObj.sc = 1;
      issInitObj.np = issOpts.np;
    }

    return issInitObj;
  } // END buildIssInitObject

  
  function logMetrics() {
    if (typeof uet == 'function' && typeof uex == 'function' ) {
      uet('be', 'iss-init-pc', {wb: 1});
      uex('ld', 'iss-init-pc', {wb: 1});
    }
  } // END logMetrics

if( window.P ){
    P.when("A").execute(function(A) {

        

        function getQueryParameterByName(name) {
            name = name.replace(/[\[]/, "\\[").replace(/[\]]/, "\\]");

            var regex = new RegExp("[\\?&]" + name + "=([^&#]*)"),
                results = regex.exec(location.search);

            return results == null ? "" : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, " "));
        }

        
        var hidden, visibilityChange;
        if (typeof document.hidden !== "undefined") { 
            hidden = "hidden";
            visibilityChange = "visibilitychange";
        } else if (typeof document.mozHidden !== "undefined") {
            hidden = "mozHidden";
            visibilityChange = "mozvisibilitychange";
        } else if (typeof document.msHidden !== "undefined") {
            hidden = "msHidden";
            visibilityChange = "msvisibilitychange";
        } else if (typeof document.webkitHidden !== "undefined") {
            hidden = "webkitHidden";
            visibilityChange = "webkitvisibilitychange";
        }

        
        var loadFeatures = function() {
            

            
            var $ = A.$,
                $container = $("#bbop-sbbop-container");

  P.when('A', 'jQuery', 'a-modal', 'a-checkbox').execute(function (A, $, modal, getCheckboxCollection) {
    //Twister agnostic vars
    var refTagPrefix = 'psd_si_';

    var buyButton;
    var buyForm;
    var serviceASIN;
    var baseASIN;
    var index;

    //cache all alternative warranty asins
    var altASINs = {};
    //cache all alternative warranty terms
    var altTerms = [];
    var selectedTerm;
    var siState;

    var updateState = function() {
      var getStateValue = function(key) {
        return siState[key] || '';
      }

      var jsonParser = function(attributeName) {
          var jsonData;
          var json = $("#" + attributeName).find('script').html();

          if (!json) {
              return null;
          }

          jsonData = $.parseJSON(json);
          return jsonData;
      }

      siState = jsonParser("PSDServicesInterstitial");
      if (siState !== undefined && siState !== null && typeof(siState) === 'object') {
          siState.baseASIN = getStateValue('baseASIN');
          siState.serviceASIN = getStateValue('serviceASIN');
          siState.serviceCanRender = getStateValue('serviceCanRender') === "true";
          siState.showInstall = getStateValue('showInstall') === "true";
          siState.expWeblab = getStateValue('expWeblab');
          siState.requestId = getStateValue('requestId');
          siState.popoverHeader = getStateValue('popoverHeader');
          siState.optoutEnabled = getStateValue('optoutEnabled') === "true";
          siState.disabledByMAP = getStateValue('disabledByMAP') === "true";
      } else {
          siState = null;
      }
    }

    var safeBuyButtonClick = function() {
      buyButton.unbind('click.siatc')                                           //Unbind the SI handler
               .click()                                                         //Trigger the ATC form submission
               .bind('click.siatc',function() {return false;});                  //Prevent additional clicks on the ATC button
    };

    var logError = function(errorMessage) {
      if (window.ueLogError) {
        var customError = { message: errorMessage };
        var additionalInfo = {
          logLevel: 'ERROR',
          attribution: 'services_interstitial_desktop'
        };
        window.ueLogError(customError, additionalInfo);
      }
    }

    var writeToUserPreferenceAndATC = function() {
      var checkbox = getCheckboxCollection('#optOutSi');
      if (checkbox.size() != 1) {
        logRefTag(refTagPrefix+"oh_"+baseASIN+"_"+serviceASIN);
        safeBuyButtonClick();
      } else if (!checkbox.isChecked()) {
        logRefTag(refTagPrefix+"on_"+baseASIN+"_"+serviceASIN);
        safeBuyButtonClick();
      } else {
        logRefTag(refTagPrefix+"oy_"+baseASIN+"_"+serviceASIN);
        A.post('/gp/si/util/opt-out.html', {
          params: {
            'sid': siState.sessionId,
            'rid': siState.requestId
          },
          success: function(data) {
            if (!data.isOK) {
              logError("Something went wrong with saving customer preferences to opt out");
            }
            safeBuyButtonClick();
          },
          error: function() {
            logError("Something went wrong with the ajax call to save customer preferences to opt out");
            safeBuyButtonClick();
          },
          timeout: 1000
        });
      }
    }

    //SI Post-Popover Display JS
    var logRefTag = function(message) {
      $.get('/gp/product/ajax-handlers/reftag.html/ref=' + message);
    };

    var bindAddHandler = function(event) {
      unbindButtonHandlers();
      logRefTag(refTagPrefix+"y_"+baseASIN+"_"+serviceASIN);
      var offeringId;
      if(typeof(selectedTerm) !== 'undefined'){
          offeringId = $('#siAddCoverage button').attr('data-offering-id-' + selectedTerm);
      }

      if(typeof(offeringId) === 'undefined'){
          offeringId = $('#siAddCoverage button').attr('data-offering-id');
      }

      var quantity = document.getElementById('quantity');
      quantity = quantity === null ? 1 : quantity.value;
      if(typeof(offeringId) !== 'undefined'){
        var buyForm = $('#addToCart');
        buyForm.append('<input type="hidden" id="useABBHandler" name="useABBHandler" value="1" />');
        buyForm.append('<input type="hidden" id="quantity.'+index+'" name="quantity.'+index+'" value="'+quantity+'" />');
        buyForm.append('<input type="hidden" id="asin.'+index+'" name="asin.'+index+'" value="'+serviceASIN+'" />');
        buyForm.append('<input type="hidden" id="offeringID.'+index+'" name="offeringID.'+index+'" value="'+offeringId+'" />');

        var itemCount =  buyForm.find('input[name="itemCount"]');
        if(itemCount.length === 0){
          buyForm.append('<input type="hidden" name="itemCount" value="'+index+'">');
        }else{
          itemCount[0].value = index;
        }
      }

      writeToUserPreferenceAndATC();
      return false;
    };

    var bindNoHandler = function() {
      unbindButtonHandlers();
      logRefTag(refTagPrefix + "n_" + baseASIN + "_" + serviceASIN);
      writeToUserPreferenceAndATC();
      return false;
    };

    var unbindButtonHandlers = function() {
      $('#siAddCoverage').unbind('click.sipopadd');
      $('#siNoCoverage').unbind('click.sipopno');
      $('#siAddCoverage').bind('click.sipopadd', function() {return false;});
      $('#siNoCoverage').bind('click.sipopno', function() {return false;});
    };

    //SI Pre-Popover Display JS

    var siBuyButtonHandler = function(){
      buyButton = $(this);
      buyForm = $('#addToCart');
      updateState();

      if (!siState || typeof siState === 'undefined') {
        return;
      }

      $(document.body).undelegate('#add-to-cart-button','click.siatc');
      
        $(document.body).undelegate('#buy-now-button', 'click.siatc');
      
      if(buyButton.length === 1 && buyForm.length === 1) {
        buyButton.bind('click.siatc', function() {return false;}); //prevent default ATC action

        index = buyForm.find("input[name^='offeringID']").length +1;

        baseASIN = siState.baseASIN;

        if (baseASIN !== null) {

          //Bind default ATC to termination of popover
          A.on('a:popover:hide:si-modal', function(event) {
              logRefTag(refTagPrefix+"n_"+baseASIN+"_"+serviceASIN);
              writeToUserPreferenceAndATC();
          });

          //Bind default ATC to AJAX failures
          A.on('a:popover:ajaxFail:si-modal', function(event) {
              safeBuyButtonClick();
          });

          
          
          
          var wbbASINs = '';
          var wbbChecks = $("#abbWrapper div").has("input[name^='offering']:checked");
          wbbChecks.find("input[name^='asin']")
                   .each(function() {wbbASINs = this.value + ',' + wbbASINs;});

          var baseOfferID = document.getElementById('offerListingID').value;
          //Request service ASIN
          A.ajax('/gp/si/util/get-services.html', {
            method: 'get',
            params: {
              asin: baseASIN,
              offerID: baseOfferID,
              limitForMAP: 1,
              abbASINs: wbbASINs,
              experimentWeblab: siState.expWeblab,
              ri: siState.requestId
            },
            success: function(data) {
              try{
                if (siState.showInstall && data.otherServices && data.otherServices.length > 1
                    && typeof data.otherServices[0]) {
                    serviceASIN = data.otherServices[0];
                }
                var serviceList = '';
                var termList = '';
                if (typeof(serviceASIN) === 'undefined' && data.services && data.services.length > 1
                    && data.services[0]){
                    serviceASIN = data.services[0];
                    if (data.filteredServices) {
                       for (var i=0; i < data.filteredServices.length-1; i++) {
                           if(data.filteredServices[i]){
                               var warrASIN = data.filteredServices[i]['asin'];
                               var warrTerm = data.filteredServices[i]['term'];
                               altASINs[warrTerm] = warrASIN;
                               altTerms.push(warrTerm);
                               if (warrASIN === serviceASIN){
                                   selectedTerm = warrTerm;
                               }
                               if (i === data.filteredServices.length-1) {
                                   serviceList += warrASIN;
                                   termList += warrTerm;
                               } else {
                                   serviceList += warrASIN + ",";
                                   termList += warrTerm + ",";
                               }
                           }
                       }
                    }
                }
                var quantity = document.getElementById('quantity');
                quantity = quantity === null ? 1 : quantity.value;
                var popupRef = refTagPrefix + 'i_' + baseASIN + '_' + serviceASIN;
                if (typeof(serviceASIN) !== 'undefined') {

                  var modalParams = {
                    "name" : "si-modal",
                    "header" : siState.popoverHeader,
                    "width" : "685"
                  };

                  modalParams["url"] = '/gp/si/aui-si-pop.html'
                                + '/ref=' + popupRef
                                + '?ie=UTF8'
                                + '&ca=' + serviceASIN
                                + '&ba=' + baseASIN
                                + '&quantity=' + quantity
                                + '&ri=' + siState.requestId
                                + '&si=' + (siState.showInstall ? '1' : '0')
                                + '&sl=' + serviceList
                                + '&tl=' + termList
                                + '&optout=' + (siState.optoutEnabled ? '1' : '0');

                  buyForm.append('<input type="hidden" id="siHasShown" name="siHasShown" value="1" />');
                  var $trigger = $('#servicesInterstitial');
                  // This is the workaround to fix issue: https://issues.amazon.com/AUI-9696
                  var siPopover = modal.create($trigger, modalParams);
                  siPopover.attrs('synchronous', true);
                  siPopover.show();

                } else {
                  if (data.siDisabledByMap) {
                    buyForm.append('<input type="hidden" id="siHasShown" name="siHasShown" value="0" />');
                  }
                  safeBuyButtonClick();
                }
              } catch(exception) {

                if (window.ueLogError) {
                  window.ueLogError(exception,{attribution : 'servicesInterstitial'});
                }
                safeBuyButtonClick();

              }
            },
            error: function() {
                safeBuyButtonClick();
            }
          });
          
          

          return false;
        }
      }

      //If siATCHandler has not returned false by this point, the default behavior of ATC button will be triggered
    };

    // Undelegate handlers before delegating them so that the same handler
    // isn't attached to root of document multiple times on Twister update.
    $(document.body).undelegate('#add-to-cart-button', 'click.siatc');
    
      $(document.body).undelegate('#buy-now-button', 'click.siatc');
    
    $(document.body).undelegate('#add-to-cart-button','click.vaswarrantysiatc');
    $(document.body).undelegate('#siAddCoverage', 'click.sipopadd');
    $(document.body).undelegate('#siNoCoverage', 'click.sipopno');
    A.off('a:button-group:si_twister_button_group:toggle');

    $(document.body).delegate('#add-to-cart-button','click.siatc', siBuyButtonHandler);
    
      $(document.body).delegate('#buy-now-button', 'click.siatc', siBuyButtonHandler);
    
    $(document.body).delegate('#siAddCoverage','click.sipopadd', bindAddHandler);
    $(document.body).delegate('#siNoCoverage','click.sipopno', bindNoHandler);

    A.on('a:button-group:si_twister_button_group:toggle', function(data) {
      $(".a-button-toggle").addClass("a-button-disabled");
      //Get the popover instance
      //Not using the button name from data.selectedButton.buttonName since this is probabaly an AUI bug
      //since sometimes it would trigger a toggle event with an undefined button name[been verfied in console]
      //var selectedTerm = data.selectedButton.buttonName;

      //Manually retrieve the selected button
      var currentTerm = $(".si_toggle_button.a-button-selected input").attr("name");
      var currentASIN = altASINs[selectedTerm];
      serviceASIN = currentASIN;
      selectedTerm = currentTerm;
      for(var i = 0; i < altTerms.length; i++){
          $(".si_pop_content_" + altTerms[i]).hide();
      }
      $(".si_pop_content_" + currentTerm).show();
      $(".a-button-toggle").removeClass("a-button-disabled");
    });
  });
',

    P.when("A", "jQuery").execute(function(A, $) {
        $("#quantity").live("change", function (event) {
            if (event.updateFTOnQuantityChange) {
                return;
            }
            event.updateFTOnQuantityChange = 1;

            var quantity = $(this).val();
            var asin = $("#ftSelectAsin").val();
            var merchantId = $("#ftSelectMerchant").val();

            if (!asin || !merchantId) {
                return;
            }

            var params = [];
            params.push("asin=" + asin);
            params.push("quantity=" + quantity);
            params.push("merchantId=" + merchantId);

            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "/gp/product/features/dp-fast-track/udp-ajax-handler/get-quantity-update-message.html?ie=UTF8",
                contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded;charset=utf-8',
                data: params.join('&'),
                dataType: "html",
                success: function(objResponse) {
                    if (objResponse != null && objResponse != "") {
                        $("#fast-track-message").replaceWith(objResponse);
                    }
                }
            });
            return;
        });
    });
',

P.when('A','jQuery').execute(function (A,$) {
    P.now('vas-uePublisher','A','jQuery').execute(function(vasUepublisher,A,$){
        if(vasUepublisher == undefined){
            P.when('A','jQuery').register('vas-uePublisher', function (A,$) {
                return {
                    metric : function(ueMetricName){
                        var prefixedMetricName = "vas_ppd_" + ueMetricName;
                        if (typeof ue !== 'undefined') {
                            if(typeof ue.count !== 'undefined')
                               ue.count(prefixedMetricName,1);
                        }                        
                    },
                    increaseMetricBy : function(ueMetricName, value){
                        var prefixedMetricName = "vas_ppd_" + ueMetricName;
                        if (typeof ue !== 'undefined') {
                            if(typeof ue.count !== 'undefined')
                               ue.count(prefixedMetricName, value);
                        }
                    },
                    log : function(exception){
                        if (window.ueLogError) {
                            var additionalInfo = { 
                                logLevel : 'ERROR',
                                attribution : 'ppd-bundles'
                            };
                            window.ueLogError(exception,additionalInfo);
                        }
                    },
                    //TODO make the below function to accept these parameters as a single object
                    logRefTag : function(refTag, pageType, subPageType, pageTypeId, hitType, merchantId, pageAsin, sdpMinimumPriceNew, merchantAsinPrice){
                        if(refTag){
                            var prefix = "?";
                            var refTagParams = "";
                            if(pageType){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "pageType="+pageType);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            if(subPageType){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "subPageType="+subPageType);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            if(pageTypeId){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "pageTypeId="+pageTypeId);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            if(hitType){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "hitType="+hitType);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }else{
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "hitType=popUp");
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            if(merchantId){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "merchantId="+merchantId);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            if(pageAsin){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "pageAsin="+pageAsin);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            if(sdpMinimumPriceNew){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "sdpMinimumPriceNew="+sdpMinimumPriceNew);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            if(merchantAsinPrice){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "merchantAsinPrice="+merchantAsinPrice);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            
                            $.get('/gp/ls/impress.html/ref=' + refTag + refTagParams);
                            
                            if (typeof ue !== 'undefined') {
                                if(typeof ue.count !== 'undefined')
                                   ue.count(refTag,1);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                };
            });
        }
    });
});
',

    P.now('A','jQuery','vas-weblab-trigger').execute(function(A,$,vasWeblabTrigger) {

            P.when('A','jQuery','ready').register('vas-weblab-trigger', function(A,$) {
                var publishMetric = function(weblabName, treatment) {
                    if (typeof ue !== 'undefined') {
                        if(typeof ue.count !== 'undefined') {
                            ue.count(weblabName + "-" + treatment,1);
                        };

                };
                return {
                    publishMetric : function(weblabName, treatment) {
                        publishMetric(weblabName, treatment);

                    triggerWeblab : function(weblabName, treatment) {
                        A.ajax('/gp/ls/vas-ajax-handlers/vas-weblab-trigger.html', {
                            method: 'get',
                            params: {
                                    weblab : weblabName,
                                    weblabTreatment : treatment
                            },
                            success: function() {
                                publishMetric(weblabName, treatment);
                            }

                        return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function(c) {
                            var r = Math.random()*16|0, v = c == 'x' ? r : (r&0x3|0x8);
                            return v.toString(16);
                        });
                    },
                };

P.when("A").execute(function(A) {
   
   function vote(event) {
     var root = A.$(event.data.rootComponentId);
     var target = event.$target;
     root.find(".cr-vote-buttons").addClass("a-hidden");
     root.find(".cr-vote-feedback").removeClass("a-hidden");
       
     A.get(target.attr("href") + "&type=json&_=" + (new Date()).getTime(),
     {
	   dataType: 'json',
	   ajaxTimeout: 10000,
	   success: function(data, textStatus){ 
         success(data, root, target);
       },
	   error: function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown){
         error(root, target);
       }
	 });
     event.$event.preventDefault();

   }

   function isNoButton(target) {       
     return target.closest(".noButton").length > 0;
   }

   function success(data, root, target) {
       if (data.redirect == 1) {
	   window.location.href = target.attr("href");
       } else if (data.error == 1) {
	   error(root, target);
       } else {
	   root.find(".cr-vote-success").removeClass("a-hidden");	   
	   root.find(".cr-vote-feedback").addClass("a-hidden");
       }
   }

   function error(root, target) {
       root.find(".cr-vote-error").removeClass("a-hidden");	   
       root.find(".cr-vote-feedback").addClass("a-hidden");
   }

   A.declarative("cr-vote", ["click"], vote);
});

This is the environment the Aura Spectrum D.I. was designed for.", CONSTRUCTION: This is a beefy and handsome device: heavy duty metal case, nonslip feet, smooth turning dials, sturdy footswitches and simple control layout. The control labels are too small to read while on the floor but no biggie once you memorize the layout. I assumed the image/patch would be displayed on the LCD but, instead, the LCD is reserved for tuner and bypass functions.', SOUND QUALITY: According to Fishman, the Aura makes an under saddle pickup sound like a studio mic. As wonderful as the undersaddle piezo pickup is, it is not exactly natural in timbre or response. It's in the ball park but has definite electronic undertones: a tendency for harshness (piezo quack), increased sustain and electronic coloration. The Aura is supposed to simulate natural acoustic tone by blending an "image" of a mic'd acoustic guitar with the pickup signal. So does it work?', My point of reference is a mix of my Neumann KM184 mic and the Cool Tubes pickup system on my Hirade TH90 and TH8SS classical guitars. Mixed 60/40 pickup and mic this combo is amazing through my Genz Benz acoustic guitar amp. I love this sound but it is a pain to carry around to gigs and it feeds back at even moderate volume.', Read more \u203a',

  function initializeAutocomplete(jQuery) {
    
    var issInitObj = buildIssInitObject(opts, issOpts);

    tryInitClientTriggeredWeblabs(issInitObj);
  } // END initializeAutocomplete

  
  
  function tryInitClientTriggeredWeblabs(issInitObj) {
    
    if (opts.isDoCtw) {
      $SearchJS.importEvent('search-csl');
      $SearchJS.when('search-csl').run('autocomplete-csl-init', function delegateToInitSearchCsl(searchCSL) { initSearchCsl( searchCSL, issInitObj ); } );
    } else {
      $SearchJS.declare('canCreateAutocomplete', issInitObj);
    }
  }

  
  
  function initSearchCsl(searchCSL, issInitObject) {
    searchCSL.init(opts.pageType, (window.ue && window.ue.rid) || opts.requestId);

    
    var keydownCtw = opts.keydownTriggeredWeblabs;
    var displayCtw = opts.displayTriggeredWeblabs;

    
    issInitObject.doCTWKeydown = function(e) {
        for (var i = 0; i < keydownCtw.length; i++) {
          searchCSL.addWlt(keydownCtw[i].call ? keydownCtw[i](e) : keydownCtw[i]);
        }
      };

    issInitObject.doCTWDisplay = function(data) {
        for (var i = 0; i < displayCtw.length; i++) {
          searchCSL.addWlt(displayCtw[i].call ? displayCtw[i](data) : displayCtw[i]);
        }
      };

    $SearchJS.declare('canCreateAutocomplete', issInitObject);
  } // END initSearchCsl

  
  
  function createAutocomplete(issObject) {
    iss = new AutoComplete(issObject);

    $SearchJS.publish('search-js-autocomplete', iss);

    logMetrics();
  } // END createAutocomplete

  
  
  function buildIssInitObject(opts, issOpts, isNewIss) {
    var issInitObj = {
        src: opts.host
      , sessionId: opts.sessionId
      , requestId: opts.requestId
      , mkt: opts.marketId
      , obfMkt: opts.obfuscatedMarketId
      , pageType: opts.pageType
      , language: opts.language
      , aliases: opts.searchAliases
      , fb: issOpts.fallbackFlag
      , isDigitalFeaturesEnabled: issOpts.isDigitalFeaturesEnabled
      , isWayfindingEnabled: issOpts.isWayfindingEnabled
      , issPrimeEligible: issOpts.issPrimeEligible
      , deptText: issOpts.departmentText
      , sugText: issOpts.suggestionText
      , filterAliases: opts.filterAliases
      , emphasizeSuggestionsTreatment: issOpts.emphasizeSuggestionsTreatment
      , crossCategoryEmphasisTreatment: issOpts.crossCategoryEmphasisTreatment
      , showSuggestionsOnSearchboxFocusTreatment: issOpts.showSuggestionsOnSearchboxFocusTreatment
      , issAfterNCharsTreatment: issOpts.issAfterNCharsTreatment
      , issRelatedSearchesTreatment: issOpts.issRelatedSearchesTreatment
      , recentSearchesTreatment: issOpts.recentSearchesTreatment
      , recentSearchesText: issOpts.recentSearchesText
      , cf: issOpts.cf
      , ime: opts.isJpOrCn
      , mktid: opts.marketId
      , qs: opts.isJpOrCn
      , issCorpus: issOpts.issCorpus
      , deepNodeISS: {
          searchAliasAccessor: function($) {
            return (window.SearchPageAccess && window.SearchPageAccess.searchAlias()) ||
                   $('select.searchSelect').children().attr('data-root-alias');
          },
          searchAliasDisplayNameAccessor: function() {
            return (window.SearchPageAccess && window.SearchPageAccess.searchAliasDisplayName());
          }
        }
    };

    // If we aren't using the new ISS then we need to add these properties
    if (!isNewIss) {
      issInitObj.dd = issOpts.dropdown; // The element with id searchDropdownBox doesn't exist in C.
      issInitObj.imeSpacing = issOpts.imeSpacing;
      issInitObj.isNavInline = 1;
      issInitObj.triggerISSOnClick = 0;
      issInitObj.sc = 1;
      issInitObj.np = issOpts.np;
    }

    return issInitObj;
  } // END buildIssInitObject

      uex('ld', 'iss-init-pc', {wb: 1});
    }
  } // END logMetrics

    P.when("A").execute(function(A) {

        

        function getQueryParameterByName(name) {
            name = name.replace(/[\[]/, "\\[").replace(/[\]]/, "\\]");

            var regex = new RegExp("[\\?&]" + name + "=([^&#]*)"),
                results = regex.exec(location.search);

            return results == null ? "" : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, " "));
        }

        
        var hidden, visibilityChange;
        if (typeof document.hidden !== "undefined") { 
            hidden = "hidden";
            visibilityChange = "visibilitychange";
        } else if (typeof document.mozHidden !== "undefined") {
            hidden = "mozHidden";
            visibilityChange = "mozvisibilitychange";
        } else if (typeof document.msHidden !== "undefined") {
            hidden = "msHidden";
            visibilityChange = "msvisibilitychange";
        } else if (typeof document.webkitHidden !== "undefined") {
            hidden = "webkitHidden";
            visibilityChange = "webkitvisibilitychange";
        }

        
        var loadFeatures = function() {
            

            
            var $ = A.$,
                $container = $("#bbop-sbbop-container");

            var data = {
                "ASIN" : "B002KWG4QA",
                "merchantID" : "ATVPDKIKX0DER",
                "bbopruleID" : "Acquisition_AddToCart_PrimeBasicFreeTrialUpsellEligible",
                "sbbopruleID" : "",
                "deliveryOptions" : "[next,second]",
                "preorder" : "false",
                "releaseDateDeliveryEligible" : "false"
            };
            var scope = "bbopAjaxCall";            
            if(typeof uet === 'function') {
                uet('bb', scope, {wb: 1});
            }
            
            $.get("/gp/product/du/bbop-ms3-ajax-endpoint.html", data, function(result) {
                
                    
                    
                        $container.append(result);
                    
                
                if(typeof uet === 'function' && typeof uex === 'function') {
                    
                    uet( "cf", scope, {wb: 1} );
                    uex( "ld", scope, {wb: 1} );
                }
                
                
                

                if (getQueryParameterByName("checkBBOP") === "true") {
                    P.when("a-modal", "ready").execute(function(modal) {
                      $('#bbop-check-box').click();
                    });
                }

                
            });

            
            
        }

        
        var handleVisibilityChange = function() {
            if (!document[hidden]) {
                
                document.removeEventListener(visibilityChange, handleVisibilityChange);
                loadFeatures();
            }
        }

        if (typeof document.addEventListener === "undefined" ||
            typeof document[hidden] === "undefined" || !document[hidden]) {
            
            loadFeatures();
        } else {
            
            document.addEventListener(visibilityChange, handleVisibilityChange);
        }
    });
}

    var $ = A.$;

    function logRefTag(refTag) {
      $.get("/gp/product/ajax-handlers/reftag.html/ref=" + refTag);
    }
    
    function hidePopover(index) {
      var popover = modal.get("mbbPopover" + index);
      if (popover != null) {
        popover.hide();
      }
    }

    function logCheckBoxRefTag(isChecked, index, warrantyAsin) {
      var suffix = (index+1) + "_B002KWG4QA_" + warrantyAsin;
      if (isChecked) {
        logRefTag("psd_bb_y" + suffix);
      } else {
        logRefTag("psd_bb_n" + suffix);
      }
    }

    $("#buybox .js-abbNew input[id^=mbb-offeringID-]").click(function() {
      var flag = this.checked;
      
      
      
        
        
          getCheckboxCollection('input[id^=mbb-offeringID-]').uncheck();
        
      
      this.checked = flag;
      var index = $('#buybox .js-abbNew input[id^=mbb-offeringID-]').index(this);
      var warrantyAsin = $(this).parents('.abbListItem').find('input[name^=asin]').val();
      logCheckBoxRefTag(flag, index, warrantyAsin);
    });

    $("#buybox #quantity").change(function() {
      var quantity = $(this).val();
      $("#buybox .js-abbNew input[name^=quantity]").each(function() {
        this.value = quantity;
       });
    });

P.when('A','jQuery').execute(function(A,$)  {
    function toggleExpanderHeaderTextWeight(data) {
       $("[data-a-expander-name="+data.expander.expanderName+"] .a-mbc-expander-heading-text").toggleClass("a-mbc-expander-heading-text-bold");
    }

    var offerCount = 3;

        });

            window.open(this.href,"_self");
        });
        A.on('a:expander:mbc_expander_'+i+':toggle:expand', toggleExpanderHeaderTextWeight);
        A.on('a:expander:mbc_expander_'+i+':toggle:collapse', toggleExpanderHeaderTextWeight);
    }

    if ($("#mbc-panel").length == 0) {
        $("#mbc-action-panel-wrapper").show();
    }

    	    ', {"serviceCanRender":"true","baseASIN":"B002KWG4QA","popoverHeader":"Add to your order","requestId":"839585VGV0R7EGKXF7ZD","disabledByMAP":"false","serviceASIN":"B01LX4JEU0","sessionId":"000-0000000-0000000","showInstall":"false","optoutEnabled":"false"}',

  P.when('A', 'jQuery', 'a-modal', 'a-checkbox').execute(function (A, $, modal, getCheckboxCollection) {
    //Twister agnostic vars
    var refTagPrefix = 'psd_si_';

    var buyButton;
    var buyForm;
    var serviceASIN;
    var baseASIN;
    var index;

    //cache all alternative warranty asins
    var altASINs = {};
    //cache all alternative warranty terms
    var altTerms = [];
    var selectedTerm;
    var siState;

    var updateState = function() {
      var getStateValue = function(key) {
        return siState[key] || '';
      }

      var jsonParser = function(attributeName) {
          var jsonData;
          var json = $("#" + attributeName).find('script').html();

          if (!json) {
              return null;
          }

          jsonData = $.parseJSON(json);
          return jsonData;
      }

      siState = jsonParser("PSDServicesInterstitial");
      if (siState !== undefined && siState !== null && typeof(siState) === 'object') {
          siState.baseASIN = getStateValue('baseASIN');
          siState.serviceASIN = getStateValue('serviceASIN');
          siState.serviceCanRender = getStateValue('serviceCanRender') === "true";
          siState.showInstall = getStateValue('showInstall') === "true";
          siState.expWeblab = getStateValue('expWeblab');
          siState.requestId = getStateValue('requestId');
          siState.popoverHeader = getStateValue('popoverHeader');
          siState.optoutEnabled = getStateValue('optoutEnabled') === "true";
          siState.disabledByMAP = getStateValue('disabledByMAP') === "true";
      } else {
          siState = null;
      }
    }

    var safeBuyButtonClick = function() {
      buyButton.unbind('click.siatc')                                           //Unbind the SI handler
               .click()                                                         //Trigger the ATC form submission
               .bind('click.siatc',function() {return false;});                  //Prevent additional clicks on the ATC button
    };

    var logError = function(errorMessage) {
      if (window.ueLogError) {
        var customError = { message: errorMessage };
        var additionalInfo = {
          logLevel: 'ERROR',
          attribution: 'services_interstitial_desktop'
        };
        window.ueLogError(customError, additionalInfo);
      }
    }

    var writeToUserPreferenceAndATC = function() {
      var checkbox = getCheckboxCollection('#optOutSi');
      if (checkbox.size() != 1) {
        logRefTag(refTagPrefix+"oh_"+baseASIN+"_"+serviceASIN);
        safeBuyButtonClick();
      } else if (!checkbox.isChecked()) {
        logRefTag(refTagPrefix+"on_"+baseASIN+"_"+serviceASIN);
        safeBuyButtonClick();
      } else {
        logRefTag(refTagPrefix+"oy_"+baseASIN+"_"+serviceASIN);
        A.post('/gp/si/util/opt-out.html', {
          params: {
            'sid': siState.sessionId,
            'rid': siState.requestId
          },
          success: function(data) {
            if (!data.isOK) {
              logError("Something went wrong with saving customer preferences to opt out");
            }
            safeBuyButtonClick();
          },
          error: function() {
            logError("Something went wrong with the ajax call to save customer preferences to opt out");
            safeBuyButtonClick();
          },
          timeout: 1000
        });
      }
    }

    //SI Post-Popover Display JS
    var logRefTag = function(message) {
      $.get('/gp/product/ajax-handlers/reftag.html/ref=' + message);
    };

    var bindAddHandler = function(event) {
      unbindButtonHandlers();
      logRefTag(refTagPrefix+"y_"+baseASIN+"_"+serviceASIN);
      var offeringId;
      if(typeof(selectedTerm) !== 'undefined'){
          offeringId = $('#siAddCoverage button').attr('data-offering-id-' + selectedTerm);
      }

      if(typeof(offeringId) === 'undefined'){
          offeringId = $('#siAddCoverage button').attr('data-offering-id');
      }

      var quantity = document.getElementById('quantity');
      quantity = quantity === null ? 1 : quantity.value;
      if(typeof(offeringId) !== 'undefined'){
        var buyForm = $('#addToCart');
        buyForm.append('<input type="hidden" id="useABBHandler" name="useABBHandler" value="1" />');
        buyForm.append('<input type="hidden" id="quantity.'+index+'" name="quantity.'+index+'" value="'+quantity+'" />');
        buyForm.append('<input type="hidden" id="asin.'+index+'" name="asin.'+index+'" value="'+serviceASIN+'" />');
        buyForm.append('<input type="hidden" id="offeringID.'+index+'" name="offeringID.'+index+'" value="'+offeringId+'" />');

        var itemCount =  buyForm.find('input[name="itemCount"]');
        if(itemCount.length === 0){
          buyForm.append('<input type="hidden" name="itemCount" value="'+index+'">');
        }else{
          itemCount[0].value = index;
        }
      }

      writeToUserPreferenceAndATC();
      return false;
    };

    var bindNoHandler = function() {
      unbindButtonHandlers();
      logRefTag(refTagPrefix + "n_" + baseASIN + "_" + serviceASIN);
      writeToUserPreferenceAndATC();
      return false;
    };

    var unbindButtonHandlers = function() {
      $('#siAddCoverage').unbind('click.sipopadd');
      $('#siNoCoverage').unbind('click.sipopno');
      $('#siAddCoverage').bind('click.sipopadd', function() {return false;});
      $('#siNoCoverage').bind('click.sipopno', function() {return false;});
    };

    //SI Pre-Popover Display JS

    var siBuyButtonHandler = function(){
      buyButton = $(this);
      buyForm = $('#addToCart');
      updateState();

      if (!siState || typeof siState === 'undefined') {
        return;
      }

      $(document.body).undelegate('#add-to-cart-button','click.siatc');
      
        $(document.body).undelegate('#buy-now-button', 'click.siatc');
      
      if(buyButton.length === 1 && buyForm.length === 1) {
        buyButton.bind('click.siatc', function() {return false;}); //prevent default ATC action

        index = buyForm.find("input[name^='offeringID']").length +1;

        baseASIN = siState.baseASIN;

        if (baseASIN !== null) {

          //Bind default ATC to termination of popover
          A.on('a:popover:hide:si-modal', function(event) {
              logRefTag(refTagPrefix+"n_"+baseASIN+"_"+serviceASIN);
              writeToUserPreferenceAndATC();
          });

          //Bind default ATC to AJAX failures
          A.on('a:popover:ajaxFail:si-modal', function(event) {
              safeBuyButtonClick();
          });

          
          
          
          var wbbASINs = '';
          var wbbChecks = $("#abbWrapper div").has("input[name^='offering']:checked");
          wbbChecks.find("input[name^='asin']")
                   .each(function() {wbbASINs = this.value + ',' + wbbASINs;});

          var baseOfferID = document.getElementById('offerListingID').value;
          //Request service ASIN
          A.ajax('/gp/si/util/get-services.html', {
            method: 'get',
            params: {
              asin: baseASIN,
              offerID: baseOfferID,
              limitForMAP: 1,
              abbASINs: wbbASINs,
              experimentWeblab: siState.expWeblab,
              ri: siState.requestId
            },
            success: function(data) {
              try{
                if (siState.showInstall && data.otherServices && data.otherServices.length > 1
                    && typeof data.otherServices[0]) {
                    serviceASIN = data.otherServices[0];
                }
                var serviceList = '';
                var termList = '';
                if (typeof(serviceASIN) === 'undefined' && data.services && data.services.length > 1
                    && data.services[0]){
                    serviceASIN = data.services[0];
                    if (data.filteredServices) {
                       for (var i=0; i < data.filteredServices.length-1; i++) {
                           if(data.filteredServices[i]){
                               var warrASIN = data.filteredServices[i]['asin'];
                               var warrTerm = data.filteredServices[i]['term'];
                               altASINs[warrTerm] = warrASIN;
                               altTerms.push(warrTerm);
                               if (warrASIN === serviceASIN){
                                   selectedTerm = warrTerm;
                               }
                               if (i === data.filteredServices.length-1) {
                                   serviceList += warrASIN;
                                   termList += warrTerm;
                               } else {
                                   serviceList += warrASIN + ",";
                                   termList += warrTerm + ",";
                               }
                           }
                       }
                    }
                }
                var quantity = document.getElementById('quantity');
                quantity = quantity === null ? 1 : quantity.value;
                var popupRef = refTagPrefix + 'i_' + baseASIN + '_' + serviceASIN;
                if (typeof(serviceASIN) !== 'undefined') {

                  var modalParams = {
                    "name" : "si-modal",
                    "header" : siState.popoverHeader,
                    "width" : "685"
                  };

                  modalParams["url"] = '/gp/si/aui-si-pop.html'
                                + '/ref=' + popupRef
                                + '?ie=UTF8'
                                + '&ca=' + serviceASIN
                                + '&ba=' + baseASIN
                                + '&quantity=' + quantity
                                + '&ri=' + siState.requestId
                                + '&si=' + (siState.showInstall ? '1' : '0')
                                + '&sl=' + serviceList
                                + '&tl=' + termList
                                + '&optout=' + (siState.optoutEnabled ? '1' : '0');

                  buyForm.append('<input type="hidden" id="siHasShown" name="siHasShown" value="1" />');
                  var $trigger = $('#servicesInterstitial');
                  // This is the workaround to fix issue: https://issues.amazon.com/AUI-9696
                  var siPopover = modal.create($trigger, modalParams);
                  siPopover.attrs('synchronous', true);
                  siPopover.show();

                } else {
                  if (data.siDisabledByMap) {
                    buyForm.append('<input type="hidden" id="siHasShown" name="siHasShown" value="0" />');
                  }
                  safeBuyButtonClick();
                }
              } catch(exception) {

                if (window.ueLogError) {
                  window.ueLogError(exception,{attribution : 'servicesInterstitial'});
                }
                safeBuyButtonClick();

              }
            },
            error: function() {
                safeBuyButtonClick();
            }
          });
          
          

          return false;
        }
      }

      //If siATCHandler has not returned false by this point, the default behavior of ATC button will be triggered
    };

    // Undelegate handlers before delegating them so that the same handler
    // isn't attached to root of document multiple times on Twister update.
    $(document.body).undelegate('#add-to-cart-button', 'click.siatc');
    
      $(document.body).undelegate('#buy-now-button', 'click.siatc');
    
    $(document.body).undelegate('#add-to-cart-button','click.vaswarrantysiatc');
    $(document.body).undelegate('#siAddCoverage', 'click.sipopadd');
    $(document.body).undelegate('#siNoCoverage', 'click.sipopno');
    A.off('a:button-group:si_twister_button_group:toggle');

    $(document.body).delegate('#add-to-cart-button','click.siatc', siBuyButtonHandler);
    
      $(document.body).delegate('#buy-now-button', 'click.siatc', siBuyButtonHandler);
    
    $(document.body).delegate('#siAddCoverage','click.sipopadd', bindAddHandler);
    $(document.body).delegate('#siNoCoverage','click.sipopno', bindNoHandler);

    A.on('a:button-group:si_twister_button_group:toggle', function(data) {
      $(".a-button-toggle").addClass("a-button-disabled");
      //Get the popover instance
      //Not using the button name from data.selectedButton.buttonName since this is probabaly an AUI bug
      //since sometimes it would trigger a toggle event with an undefined button name[been verfied in console]
      //var selectedTerm = data.selectedButton.buttonName;

      //Manually retrieve the selected button
      var currentTerm = $(".si_toggle_button.a-button-selected input").attr("name");
      var currentASIN = altASINs[selectedTerm];
      serviceASIN = currentASIN;
      selectedTerm = currentTerm;
      for(var i = 0; i < altTerms.length; i++){
          $(".si_pop_content_" + altTerms[i]).hide();
      }
      $(".si_pop_content_" + currentTerm).show();
      $(".a-button-toggle").removeClass("a-button-disabled");
    });
  });
',

P.when('A').register("ImageBlockATF", function(A){

    P.when("A", "jQuery").execute(function(A, $) {
        $("#quantity").live("change", function (event) {
            if (event.updateFTOnQuantityChange) {
                return;
            }
            event.updateFTOnQuantityChange = 1;

            var quantity = $(this).val();
            var asin = $("#ftSelectAsin").val();
            var merchantId = $("#ftSelectMerchant").val();

            if (!asin || !merchantId) {
                return;
            }

            var params = [];
            params.push("asin=" + asin);
            params.push("quantity=" + quantity);
            params.push("merchantId=" + merchantId);

            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "/gp/product/features/dp-fast-track/udp-ajax-handler/get-quantity-update-message.html?ie=UTF8",
                contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded;charset=utf-8',
                data: params.join('&'),
                dataType: "html",
                success: function(objResponse) {
                    if (objResponse != null && objResponse != "") {
                        $("#fast-track-message").replaceWith(objResponse);
                    }
                }
            });
            return;
        });
    });

            P.when('A','jQuery').register('vas-uePublisher', function (A,$) {
                return {
                    metric : function(ueMetricName){
                        var prefixedMetricName = "vas_ppd_" + ueMetricName;
                        if (typeof ue !== 'undefined') {
                            if(typeof ue.count !== 'undefined')
                               ue.count(prefixedMetricName,1);
                        }                        
                    },
                    increaseMetricBy : function(ueMetricName, value){
                        var prefixedMetricName = "vas_ppd_" + ueMetricName;
                        if (typeof ue !== 'undefined') {
                            if(typeof ue.count !== 'undefined')
                               ue.count(prefixedMetricName, value);
                        }
                    },
                    log : function(exception){
                        if (window.ueLogError) {
                            var additionalInfo = { 
                                logLevel : 'ERROR',
                                attribution : 'ppd-bundles'
                            };
                            window.ueLogError(exception,additionalInfo);
                        }
                    },
                    //TODO make the below function to accept these parameters as a single object
                    logRefTag : function(refTag, pageType, subPageType, pageTypeId, hitType, merchantId, pageAsin, sdpMinimumPriceNew, merchantAsinPrice){
                        if(refTag){
                            var prefix = "?";
                            var refTagParams = "";
                            if(pageType){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "pageType="+pageType);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            if(subPageType){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "subPageType="+subPageType);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            if(pageTypeId){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "pageTypeId="+pageTypeId);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            if(hitType){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "hitType="+hitType);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }else{
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "hitType=popUp");
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            if(merchantId){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "merchantId="+merchantId);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            if(pageAsin){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "pageAsin="+pageAsin);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            if(sdpMinimumPriceNew){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "sdpMinimumPriceNew="+sdpMinimumPriceNew);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            if(merchantAsinPrice){
                                refTagParams += (prefix + "merchantAsinPrice="+merchantAsinPrice);
                                prefix = "&";
                            }
                            
                            $.get('/gp/ls/impress.html/ref=' + refTag + refTagParams);
                            
                            if (typeof ue !== 'undefined') {
                                if(typeof ue.count !== 'undefined')
                                   ue.count(refTag,1);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                };
            });
        }
    });

P.when("A").execute(function(A) {
   
   function vote(event) {
     var root = A.$(event.data.rootComponentId);
     var target = event.$target;
     root.find(".cr-vote-buttons").addClass("a-hidden");
     root.find(".cr-vote-feedback").removeClass("a-hidden");
       
     A.get(target.attr("href") + "&type=json&_=" + (new Date()).getTime(),
     {
	   dataType: 'json',
	   ajaxTimeout: 10000,
	   success: function(data, textStatus){ 
         success(data, root, target);
       },
	   error: function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown){
         error(root, target);
       }
	 });
     event.$event.preventDefault();

   }

   function isNoButton(target) {       
     return target.closest(".noButton").length > 0;
   }

   function success(data, root, target) {
       if (data.redirect == 1) {
	   window.location.href = target.attr("href");
       } else if (data.error == 1) {
	   error(root, target);
       } else {
	   root.find(".cr-vote-success").removeClass("a-hidden");	   
	   root.find(".cr-vote-feedback").addClass("a-hidden");
       }
   }

   function error(root, target) {
       root.find(".cr-vote-error").removeClass("a-hidden");	   
       root.find(".cr-vote-feedback").addClass("a-hidden");
   }

   A.declarative("cr-vote", ["click"], vote);
});

var precacheDetailImages = function(imageUrls, pids) {

  function transformUrl(imgUrl, pid) {
    var suffix         = '._SL500_AA300_.jpg',
        defaultApparel = '._AA300_.jpg',
        imgUrlSplit    = imgUrl.split("._");

    if (imgUrlSplit.length) {
      var prefix = imgUrlSplit[0];
      if ((!pid  && storeName == "books") || pid == "books_display_on_website") {
        if (imgUrl.match("PIsitb-sticker-arrow")){
          var OUID = imgUrl.substr(imgUrl.indexOf('_OU'), 6);
          var lookInsideSticker = '._BO2,204,203,200_PIsitb-sticker-arrow-click,TopRight,35,-76_AA300_SH20'+ OUID +'.jpg';
          urls.push(prefix + lookInsideSticker);
        } else {
          urls.push(prefix + suffix);
        }
      } else if ((!pid && storeName == "apparel") || pid == "apparel_display_on_website") {
          urls.push(prefix + "._SX342_.jpg");
          urls.push(prefix + "._SY445_.jpg");
      } else if ((!pid && storeName == "shoes") || pid == "shoes_display_on_website") {
          urls.push(prefix + "._SX395_.jpg");
          urls.push(prefix + "._SY395_.jpg");
      } else {
        urls.push(prefix + suffix);
      }
    }
  };

  var urls = [],
      numImgsPreload = Math.min(6, imageUrls.length),
      storeName = "musical-instruments";

  for (var i = 0; i < numImgsPreload; i++){
    var currPid = (pids && pids.length) ? pids[i] : "";
    transformUrl(imageUrls[i], currPid);
  }

  for (var j = 0; j < urls.length; j++) {
    var img = new Image();
    img.src = urls[j];
  }

    var win = jQuery(window);
    var feature = jQuery("#purchaseShvl");
    var shvlPresent = feature.length > 0 ? 1:0;
    var lastCheck = 0;
    var pending = 0;
    
    var onScrollPrecache = function() {
      if (pending) {
        return; 
      }
      var lastCheckDiff = new Date().getTime() - lastCheck;
      var checkDelay = (lastCheckDiff < 200 ? 200 - lastCheckDiff : 10);
      pending = 1;
      var u = function() {
        if(shvlPresent && (win.scrollTop() + win.height() > feature.offset().top + 200)) {  
          var p = precacheDetailImages,
              $ = jQuery;
          if (p) {
            var selector = "#purchaseButtonWrapper";
            var imgElems = $(selector).find("a > div > img");
            var pgs, imgs = [], i = imgElems.length;
            while (i-- > 0) {
              imgs[i] = $(imgElems[i]).attr('src');
            }
            p(imgs,pgs);
          }
          // unbind listening on scroll once pre-caching completed
          $(window).unbind('scroll', onScrollPrecache); 
          return;
        }
        pending = 0; //precache not execute yet, wait next invoke
        lastCheck = new Date().getTime();
      };
      setTimeout(u, checkDelay);
      return;
    };
    
    jQuery(window).bind('scroll', onScrollPrecache);
